        self.grace_monitor = GraceFieldSensor()

        current_psi = self.psi_tracker.get_current_state()
        grace_field = self.grace_monitor.current_field_strength()

            action_scores[action] = future_coherence
        
        return max(action_scores, key=action_scores.get)
